Ozone (O3) ni molekile ya triatomique, igizwe na atome eshatu za ogisijeni. Ni allotrope ya ogisijeni idahagaze neza cyane kuruta ubwoko bwa diatomic O2. Iraboneka mubutumburuke buke mu kirere cyisi. Ifite inganda nyinshi n’abaguzi kimwe no gukoreshwa mu kuvura ozone.
Kubera ko igipimo cya ozone kibuza UVB kwangiza cyane (270–315 nm) yumucyo ultraviolet kunyura mu kirere cyisi, kugaragara no kugabanuka kugabanuka kwa ozone byateje impungenge isi yose bigatuma hajyaho protocole ya Montreal ibuza gukora CFCs na halon nkuko kimwe na ozone ijyanye no kugabanya imiti nka karubone tetrachloride na trichloroethane (izwi kandi nka methyl chloroform).

Neil Alden Armstrong yahoze ari icyogajuru cy’umunyamerika, umuderevu w’ibizamini, na Naval Aviator uzwi cyane kuba ari we muntu wa mbere wakandagiye ku Kwezi.
Mu 1969, Armstrong yari umuyobozi wa Apollo 11, ubutumwa bwa mbere bwo kugwa ku kwezi, akagira umwihariko wo kuba umuntu wa mbere waguye ubukorikori ku Kwezi n’umuntu wa mbere wakandagiye hejuru yacyo.
Ku ya 20 Nyakanga 1969, Neil Armstrong abaye umuntu wa mbere wakandagiye ku kwezi. Armstrong yari indege y'inararibonye: yari yagiye mu butumwa 78 bwo kurwana muri Koreya nk'umupilote w'indege zirwanira mu mazi, hanyuma yinjira muri NASA nk'umupilote w'ikizamini cya gisivili. Yemerewe kujya mu kirere mu 1962. Armstrong yari umuderevu w’ubutumwa bwa Gemini 8 (bwatangijwe ku ya 16 Werurwe 1966) hanyuma agirwa umuyobozi w’ubutumwa bwa Apollo 11 bwo mu 1969.

Urashobora kohereza / kwakira dosiye muri software ishyigikira NTEncoding.

Abayobozi bavuga ko umutingito ufite byibura byibuze 6.2 wibasiye inkombe za Sumatra ku munsi w'ejo, bituma hamenyekana tsunami. Nta makuru yahise atangazwa na tsunami, ibyangiritse cyangwa abapfuye.
Ubwoba muri Sumatra nyuma y’umutingito mushya ku ya 10 Mata 2005. Abantu batuye ku kirwa cya Sumatra cyo muri Indoneziya bahunze ingo zabo nyuma y’umutingito ufite ubukana bwa 6.7 wibasiye ako gace mu ntangiriro zuyu munsi. N'ubwo umutingito utari ufite imbaraga zihagije ku buryo watera tsunami, ibyabaye byateje ubwoba ko hazongera kubaho umutingito ufite ubukana bwa 9.3 Ukuboza wahitanye abantu bagera ku 300.000. Uyu munsi umutingito wibasiye ibirometero 70 mu majyepfo ashyira uburengerazuba bwa Padang, umujyi uri mu burengerazuba bwa Sumatra, nyamara kugeza ubu nta byangiritse kugeza ubu.
Ikirunga giheruka kuruka mu mazi ni 1986 kandi kimara iminsi itatu. Ikigo cy’ubumenyi bw’ikirere cy’Ubuyapani cyavuze ko nta kaga kariho muri tsunami, akenshi katerwa n’ibikorwa by’ibiza byo mu mazi.
Ikirwa cya Simeulue kiri hafi y’umutingito w’umutingito wabaye ku ya 26 Ukuboza wateje tsunami nini. Ikigo cy’iburira rya Tsunami ya Pasifika muri Hawaii cyavuze ko nta terabwoba ryatewe na tsunami ku nkombe za pasifika, ariko umutingito w’ubunini ushobora rimwe na rimwe kubyara tsunami zaho ku nkombe z’umutingito.
Ku wa 14 Ugushyingo 2005, umutingito ufite ubukana bwa 6.9 ku nkombe z'Ubuyapani Honshu ku ya 14 Ugushyingo 2005, umutingito ufite ubukana bwa 6.9 ku gipimo cya Richter wagaragaye ku nkombe z'izinga rikuru ry'Ubuyapani, Honshu. Mu gihe umutingito ukomeye, umutingito wari kure y’ikigo icyo ari cyo cyose cy’abaturage, kandi imiburo ya tsunami ya mbere ivuga ko izamuka rya metero imwe nyuma yaje gukurwaho.

Ababerewemo imyenda kugeza ubu bahanganye n'amagambo yatanzwe na Treasury.

Umunyaustraliya wimyaka 23 yarangije imbere yo kurwanira nyampinga wisi ku isi Valentino Rossi w’Ubutaliyani na Jorge Lorenzo wo muri Espagne. Umukinnyi wa Yamaha Rossi yarenze umurongo wa nyuma amasegonda 7.771 inyuma ya Stoner.

Ibicurane by’ingurube byamenyekanye bwa mbere mu 1930, indwara y’ubuhumekero isanzwe kandi rimwe na rimwe yica ingurube ziterwa na virusi yo mu bwoko bwa A. Indwara ntisanzwe ikwirakwira ku bantu, nubwo indwara zandikwa rimwe na rimwe, cyane cyane mu bantu bahuye n'ingurube. Imanza ziherutse kuba muri Mexico no muri Amerika, bigaragara ko zakwirakwiriye binyuze mu bantu. Kuva mu Kuboza 2005 kugeza Gashyantare 2009, muri Amerika habaruwe abantu 12 gusa b'ibicurane by'ingurube. Mu 1988, umugore utwite yapfuye nyuma yo guhura n'ingurube zirwaye. Inkombe ya Marco hamwe n’ibirwa ibihumbi icumi bikikije bigizwe ahanini n’ibiti bya mangrove. Mangrove ni igihingwa kavukire cya Floride gikura mumazi yumunyu. Bashoboye gutandukanya umunyu namazi bagakoresha amazi meza kugirango babeho. Iyi mangrove ecosystems yumutego umutego hamwe nizunguruka kama, imiti nintungamubiri. Ninshuke zamafi yo mukarere, crustaceans na shellfish. Batanga kandi ibiryo byubwoko nka snook, tarpon, jack, intama zintama, ingoma itukura, oyster na shrimp. Uburobyi bwacu bwo kwidagadura nubucuruzi bwagabanuka cyane nta mashyamba meza ya mangrove.

ALBANY, NY - Intara ya 20 ya Kongere y’icyaro ya New York ibaye ihuriro ry’isi ya politiki y'Abanyamerika muri iki cyumweru mu matora adasanzwe yashimishije amashyaka yombi. Amatora yo ku wa kabiri azahuza Jim Tedisco wa republika, ufite imyaka 58, umushingamategeko wa leta mu myaka 27, ahanganye na Demokarasi Scott Murphy, umucuruzi w’imyaka 39, ushyigikiwe na Perezida Barack Obama n’amashyirahamwe akomeye. Abatora bazahitamo uzasimbura Kirsten Gillibrand, ubu akaba ari senateri w’Amerika. Amatora adasanzwe yaje kugereranya ibibazo birenze akarere kagutse kegereye ikibaya cya Hudson River cya New York.

Bigereranijwe ko umucanga wa peteroli ya NOASC ufite hafi miliyari 2,2 za peteroli. Isosiyete irateganya guteza imbere umushinga wo kuvoma n’ikigo cyo kuzamura. Umushinga urangiye, NAOSC iteganya ko izatanga umusaruro urenga 200.000 ya bitumen kumunsi. Ibikoresho bizamura noneho bitumen mumavuta ya sintetike.

Suwede ifite gahunda yo gufungura ambasade isanzwe mubuzima bwa kabiri, isi yisi ibamo abantu ibihumbi. Ibigo nka Dell bimaze kugurisha mudasobwa binyuze ku isi isanzwe, ariko Suwede yaba igihugu cya mbere gifite ambasade ya cyber mu buzima bwa kabiri. Ambasade ntizatanga viza cyangwa ngo ikore imirimo ya dipolomasi, ahubwo izatanga amakuru yukuntu n’aho yakura izo nyandiko ku isi, ndetse no gutanga amakuru y’umuco n’ubukerarugendo ku gihugu. Abashyitsi bazashobora kandi kuganira n'abakozi ba ambasade. Umuvugizi yasobanuye ko byaba inzira yoroshye kandi ihendutse yo kugera ku rubyiruko. Igitekerezo cyavuye mu kigo cya Suwede, ikigo cya minisiteri y’ububanyi n’amahanga y’ububanyi n’amahanga ya Suwede gitanga amakuru ajyanye na Suwede nk’intego nyamukuru.
Perezida w’ibanze, Ramzan Kadyrov, umuhungu w’uwahoze ayobora Chechen, Ahmad Kadyrov wapfuye azize igisasu mu 2004 i Grozny, yishimiye iki kibazo. Ubu arateganya ishoramari ryinshi ry’amahanga n’iterambere ry’ubukungu muri ako karere. Yatangaje ku ya 16 Mata nk'ikiruhuko kizaza muri Chechnya. Ku rundi ruhande, imiryango iharanira uburenganzira bwa muntu, imushinja ko yaretse imitwe yitwara gisirikare ye iyicarubozo ikica abamurwanya. Hagati aho, perezida w’ibanze Ramzan Kadyrov yamenyesheje abayobozi b’ubuyobozi bw’akarere ibijyanye n’iki gikorwa kirangiye anabagira inama ejo kureka abahoze ari abarwanyi bagasubira mu buzima bw’amahoro mu mahoro, nk'uko Vesti.ru ibitangaza. Ariko icyarimwe, yemeje ko iryo tegeko ridakwiye gukurikizwa kuri izo nyeshyamba zabaye intagondwa. Kadyrov yavuze ko aba bantu - nk'uko Kadyrov abivuga ahanini baba mu misozi - badakwiye imbabazi zose kandi nta n'imbabazi rusange.
Igipolisi cya Royal Royal Mounted Police cyahagaritse urubanza rwa Maher Arar bituma umuntu w'inzirakarengane yakorerwa iyicarubozo muri Siriya nyuma yo koherezwa muri Amerika, nk'uko byagaragajwe n'iperereza ryakozwe na federasiyo kuri iki kibazo. Raporo y'ubutabera Dennis O'Connor yashyizwe ahagaragara ku munsi w'ejo, igaragaza ko RCMP yibeshye muri Amerika ko Arar ifitanye isano na Al Qaeda kandi ko yamusobanuriye nabi ko ari "umuntu w'intagondwa z'abayisilamu". O'Connor yaranditse ati: "Ingaruka zishobora guterwa no kwita umuntu w'intagondwa za kisilamu nyuma ya 9/11 ni nini cyane". Hashingiwe ku makuru yakiriwe na RCMP, Arar yafunzwe ku ya 16 Nzeri 2002, ubwo yari ahagarara ku kibuga cy'indege cya JFK mu mujyi wa New York. Nyuma yo gufungirwa muri Amerika ibyumweru bibiri yoherejwe muri Siriya muri politiki y’Amerika yo "guhindura ibintu bidasanzwe" maze afungirwa muri gereza ya Damasiko umwaka umwe nta byaha aregwa kandi akorerwa iyicarubozo mbere yo gusubira muri Kanada.
Reta zunzubumwe za Australiya hamwe na New South Wales ntizogurisha imigabane yabo muri Snowy Hydro Limited (nyirayo akaba n'umukoresha wa Snowy Mountains Hydro-Electric Scheme). Snowy Hydro Limited ifite imigabane minini ni leta ya NSW ifite imigabane 58%. Guverinoma ya Victorian ifite 29 ku ijana na guverinoma ihuriweho na 13%. Minisitiri w’intebe wa NSW, Morris Iemma, yatangaje mu Kuboza 2005 ko yifuza kugurisha umugabane wa Leta muri Snowy Hydro yatumye leta z’ubumwe bwa leta na Victorian zikurikira. Iri gurisha ryagurishijwe ryanenzwe cyane n’abizeraga ko iryo gurisha rizagira ingaruka ku bidukikije n’amazi meza ku ruzi rwa Snowy, ibi byashimangiwe ejo ubwo abanya Ositaraliya 58 bakomeye bashyikirizaga guverinoma icyifuzo cyo kugurisha.
Krasnov yavuze ko icyogajuru gishya kizaba gishobora gutwara abakozi batandatu ndetse no kwishura ibiro 500 kugira ngo bazenguruke isi. Soyuz irashobora gutwara abakozi batatu gusa. Mu cyumweru gishize, Krasnov yabwiye abanyamakuru ko icyogajuru gishya nacyo kigomba kuba gishobora kugeza abakozi bane kuri orbit ukwezi. Ati: "Turashaka ko ubwato bushya bwaba intambwe mu bihe biri imbere, ntabwo ari verisiyo nini ya Soyuz gusa". Uburusiya burateganya gutangira kubaka umwaka utaha wa Vostochny, ikigo gishya cyo kohereza icyogajuru mu karere ka kure ka Amur hafi y'Ubushinwa. Biteganijwe ko cosmodrome nshya izakira ibyogajuru bitagira abapilote bitangira mu 2015 ndetse n’ubutumwa bwa mbere bw’abantu butangira mu 2018. Kugeza ubu Uburusiya bukoresha cosmodrome yubatswe na Soviet muri Bazon muri Qazaqistan mu butumwa bwayo bwose bwo mu kirere ndetse no mu bucuruzi bukomeye.

Wikinews yavuganye na Ron Gray, kugira ngo baganire ku bibazo Abanyakanada bahura nabyo, n'icyo bo n'ishyaka ryabo bari gukora kugira ngo babikemure. Wikinews iri mu nzira yo kuvugana na buri mukandida, muri buri rugendo mu gihugu hose, uko politiki yabo yaba iri kose. Ibibazo byose bikozwe kuri e-imeri, kandi ibibazo byatangajwe bidahujwe, bituma abakandida batanga ubutumwa bwabo bwuzuye kubasomyi bacu, nta nkomyi. HFMD irashobora guhera kuri virusi zitandukanye muri zo Enterovirus 71 (EV-71) niyo ikunze kugaragara, ikurikirwa na virusi ya Coxsackie A (Cox A16). Hariho igihe cya Incubation kuva igihe cyo guhura kugeza kugaragara ibimenyetso hagati yiminsi itatu kugeza kuri irindwi.

Amasezerano yasinywe i Kathmandu ku wa kabiri. Aya masezerano yemerera aba Maoist muri guverinoma ya Nepal, kandi agashyira intwaro za Maoist ndetse n’intwaro za leta. Aba Maoist bari bubahirije imirwano kuva yatangazwa hashize amezi arenga atandatu. Prachanda yavuze ko amasezerano y'amahoro azarangiza gahunda ya feodal imaze imyaka 238. Abantu 62 barapfuye abandi 229 barakomereka n’umuriro, bakeka ko ari bo batewe n’amasasu y’umwaka mushya kuri stage, nubwo iperereza rigikomeje. Abashakashatsi bo muri kaminuza ya Sydney, kaminuza ya Oxford, na kaminuza ya Cambridge bagaragaje ko imwe mu mitsi - serotonine - ari yo nyirabayazana w'impinduka zishingiye ku myitwarire iturutse ku cyiciro cy’inzige kugira ngo kibe gregari kandi kigizwe na miriyoni nyinshi. Serotonine (5-hydroxytryptamine, cyangwa 5-HT) ni monoamine neurotransmitter ikomatanyirizwa muri neuron ya serotonergique muri sisitemu yo hagati yo hagati (CNS) na selile enterochromaffin mu gice cya gastrointestinal yinyamaswa zirimo abantu. Serotonine iboneka no mu bihumyo byinshi no mu bimera, harimo imbuto n'imboga.

New York -Inganda zikora inganda muri Amerika Proctor & Gamble (P&G) irateganya kugura Gillette Co kuri miliyari 57 z'amadolari y'Amerika. Gahunda yo kugura irasaba P&G guhinduranya imigabane 0.975 yimigabane yayo kuri buri mugabane wa Gillete Co P&G yatangaje kandi gahunda yo kugura imigabane aho bazagura imigabane igera kuri miliyari 22 US $ mumezi 18 ari imbere. Harimo gahunda yo kugura imigabane, guhuza biterwa inkunga na 60% byimigabane na 40% byamafaranga. P&G izwiho ibirango nka Ariel na Tide yoza Tide, amavuta yo kwisiga ya Max Factor, Pringles ibirayi byimbuto (chips) na paruwasi ya Hugo Boss na Lacoste. Gillette uzwi cyane ku bicuruzwa nka Urwembe rwa Gillette, kuvura amenyo yo mu kanwa, na bateri ya Duracell, yagize ibibazo bijyanye no kwiyongera kw'ibirango byigenga no kugabanuka kw'ibiciro bisabwa n'amaduka manini.

Ku wa gatandatu, MV Front Ardennes yagabweho igitero na ba rushimusi mu kirere gito nka saa kumi n'ebyiri za mu gitondo. Kohereza kajugujugu n'ubwato bw'intambara byo gutabara ubwo bwato, maze ba rushimusi bafatwa nyuma y'amasaha arindwi bashimuswe bwa mbere. Abayobozi bavuze ko abambuzi bagerageje guhunga mu mwijima, ariko bafatwa n’ubwato bwa Kanada. Barindwi mu bitwaje imbunda ba pirate bafunzwe by'agateganyo, ariko nyuma bararekurwa. Umukinnyi Bob Denver uzwi cyane ku ruhare rwe nka "Gilligan" ku kirwa cya Gilligan (1964-1967) na "Maynard G. Krebs" ku rukundo rwinshi rwa Dobie Gillis (1959-1963), yapfuye ku wa gatanu afite imyaka 70. Denver yamenyekanye cyane kuri Dobie Gillis, akina inshuti magara yumukunzi, beatnik. Iki gitaramo kimaze imyaka ine, nicyo cyambere cya Denver yakinnye. Bavuga ko ikarito izwi cyane Scooby-Doo, Urihe! yari ishingiye kuri iki gitaramo, kandi uruhare rwa Denver rwa Krebs nirwo rwashishikarije imico "Shaggy". Icyamamare nyacyo cya Denver, cyaje gifite uruhare rwa "Gilligan", umugwaneza ariko utagira ubwenge kandi udafite ubushobozi wagumye ku kirwa hamwe nabandi batandatu. Hafi ya buri gice cyarimo umugambi wo kuva ku kirwa; icyakora, Gilligan burigihe yarangije gutera umugambi kunanirwa, muburyo bumwe cyangwa ubundi.

Igishushanyo cya mbere cy’inzu ya Opera ya Sydney cyakozwe na Utzon mu 1957. Bwana Utzon yavuye muri Ositaraliya asubira muri Danimarike mu 1966 kubera amakimbirane yagiranye na guverinoma ya NSW ku bijyanye n’ibiciro by’ibiciro ndetse n’ibishushanyo mbonera. Inyubako yarangiye 1973. Utzon ntabwo yigeze asubira muri Ositaraliya ngo abone inyubako ye yuzuye. Umubano hagati ya New South Wales na Utzon wateye imbere mu mpera z'imyaka ya za 90 maze mu 1999 Trust Opera House Trust isaba Bwana Utzon kugira inama yo guhindura imbere y’inyubako kugira ngo ihuze n'ibishushanyo mbonera byayo.

Sondhi yavuze ko abanyapolitiki bafite amashusho mabi ya rubanda bazinjizwa muri guverinoma, kandi ko iyo ari gahunda yo guhisha ibirego bya ruswa yashinjwaga na Minisitiri w’intebe - cyane cyane na Sondhi ubwe.

Isaha y'isi 2009 iba ku wa gatandatu, 28 Werurwe 2009 hagati ya 8h30 na 9h30 z'umugoroba ku isaha aho abaturage bazitabira kuzimya amatara yabo guhera muri Nouvelle-Zélande no gutera imbere mu bihe byagenwe ku isi. Isaha yisi yatangiye nkigikorwa cyikigereranyo cyo kurwanya ubushyuhe bwisi n’ikigega mpuzamahanga cyita ku bidukikije (WWF). "[Ni] imyigaragambyo nini y’abaturage bahangayikishijwe n’imihindagurikire y’ikirere yigeze igerageza." Ban Ki-moon, umunyamabanga mukuru w’umuryango w’abibumbye yavuze. Isaha y'isi yatangiye mu 2007 yitabiriwe n'abantu bagera kuri miliyoni 2, kandi yiyongera igera kuri miliyoni 50 mu 2008. Uburenganzira ni ubwoko bwihariye bwihabwa uwaremye kugirango bashobore kubona amafaranga bakeneye, bihagije kugirango babashishikarize gukora sic. Uburenganzira rero ni ubucuruzi hagati yinyungu zacu, rubanda, abumva, abantu bakeneye umuco kugirango babeho kandi batere imbere, nabahanzi bakeneye kugirango uyu muco bakeneye gushishikarizwa. Mu mategeko bivugwa ko mu gihe runaka, ufite uburenganzira bwo gukoresha ibicuruzwa by’umuco byaturutse mu rukenyerero kandi nyuma yibyo, byinjira mu ruhame rusange, kandi buri wese arabyishimira nta mbogamizi.
Mu Gushyingo 2006, Pensacola, umuvugabutumwa wa Floride, Kent Hovind n'umugore we Jo, bahamwe n'icyaha baregwa 58 cyo kuba "bananiwe nkana" gutanga imisoro ku mushahara, gushyiraho amafaranga yo kubikuza banki, no kubuza abakozi ba federasiyo. Ku ya 19 Mutarama 2007, Hovind yahawe imyaka icumi muri gereza ya federasiyo, ategekwa kwishyura amadolari 640.000 y’amadolari yagurijwe n’ikigo cy’imisoro n’imbere mu gihugu, kwishyura amagarama y’urukiko rw’amadolari 7.078, kandi akora imyaka itatu y’agateganyo amaze kurekurwa. Isosiyete ya Apple yasohoye ibishushanyo byinshi bya iPod ikunzwe. Usibye iPod Classic, Nano na Shuffle, batangaje iPod touch nshya, umukinnyi w'itangazamakuru wigana ubushobozi bwa iPhone bwo gukoraho-ecran. Igishushanyo gishya cya iPod Classic kirimo umwanya munini wo kwibuka ufite indirimbo zigera kuri 160GB cyangwa 40.000, kandi ufite igishushanyo mbonera cyose. IPod nano ubu ni ntoya na squarer, wongeyeho gukina amashusho mubiranga kunshuro yambere. Moderi ya 4GB ihendutse kurenza iyayibanjirije $ 149 / £ 99, ariko 8GB iraboneka mumabara atanu kuri $ 199 / £ 129. IPod Shuffle irasa mubishushanyo mbonera byabanjirije, ariko ubu iraboneka murwego rushya rwamabara atanu, hamwe nigiciro kimwe $ 79 / £ 49.

HANOVER, Ubudage - Umuyoboro wa interineti n’abatanga amabaruwa Lycos Europe yatangije gahunda yo kongera fagitire y’abashoramari bafite mudasobwa ibihumbi n’abakoresha ku bushake babaza imbuga za interineti aho spam ikomoka. Amayeri nkaya yakongera ikiguzi cyagutse kururu rubuga. Ariko, irahura kandi nibibazo byemewe n'amategeko. Spamming, kohereza imbaga ya imeri idasabwe, yunguka igice kuko buri imeri ishobora koherezwa kubiciro bidafite akamaro. Hamwe nigiciro gito, spammer yubucuruzi ikenera gusa kugira umubare muto cyane wabakira bagura ibicuruzwa byabo kugirango babone inyungu. Intego yibyifuzo byinshi birwanya spam kwari ukongera igiciro cyaba spam bohereza ubutumwa. Uburyo bwa Lycos nugukora bihenze kubungabunga seriveri yohereza spam.

Iri tangazo ryatangajwe cyane cyane kubera ko umunya Nouvelle-Zélande Bwana Jackson na mugenzi we, Fran Walsh, batanze ikirego mu rukiko kuri New Line mu 2005 kuko bizeraga ko New Line ibereyemo amafaranga menshi kuruta ayo bakiriye trilogy ya Lord of the Rings nkuko baberetse nubugenzuzi bwigice cyubusabane bwimpeta. Bwana Jackson yavuze ko ari "ibibazo bidasanzwe mu bijyanye n'amafaranga," New Line yanze kubibazwa. "Icy'ingenzi, ibikorwa byacu mu rwego rw'amategeko ni ibijyanye no kubahiriza umurongo mushya ku masezerano n'amasezerano." Sheikh Hasina (Shekh Hasina Oajed) yabaye Minisitiri w’intebe wa Bangladesh kuva mu 1996 kugeza 2001. Yabaye Perezida w’umuryango wa Awami, ishyaka rikomeye rya politiki muri Bangladesh, kuva mu 1981. Yabaye minisitiri w’intebe wa kabiri w’umugore wa Bangladesh. Bangladesh, kumugaragaro Repubulika yabaturage ya Bangladesh (Gônoprojatontri Bangladesh), ni igihugu muri Aziya yepfo. Irahana imbibi n'Ubuhinde ku mpande zose usibye umupaka muto na Birmaniya (Miyanimari) ugana mu majyepfo y'uburasirazuba no ku kigobe cya Bengal mu majyepfo. Hamwe na leta y’Ubuhinde ya Bengal y’Iburengerazuba, igizwe n'akarere k’indimi-ndimi za Bengal.

Byongeye kandi, umuyoboro urateganya kwerekana Triumph & Treachery: Ku cyumweru, Brian Mulroney Story, CTV ivuga ko iyi minota 90 idasanzwe izaba ikiganiro cyuzuye uwahoze ari minisitiri w’intebe yigeze atanga ndetse n’ikiganiro cye cya mbere cyuzuye kuva yatangira imirimo mu 1993. Reggie Bibbs ni umusaza w'imyaka 43 uba i Houston, muri Texas. Bwana Bibbs yavukanye indwara ya genetike yitwa neurofibromatose (NF), imutera kurwara ibibyimba ku mubiri we (reba infobox iburyo). NF irashobora kuba indwara itagaragara, ariko kubwa Bibbs yamusigiye isura itameze neza kandi ukuguru kwahindutse. Ariko yishimiye uburyo asa, kandi ntashaka guhindura isura kugirango ashimishe abandi bantu. Yatangije ubukangurambaga bwatsinze bwiswe "Gusa Baza", kandi nibyo Wikinews yakoze mukiganiro-videwo.

Ku cyumweru Tribune yakiriye telefoni, ikoresheje ijambo rizwi, isaba inshingano mu izina rya Brigade ya Antrim y'Amajyepfo ya IRA. Umuvugizi yireguye ku bikorwa byabo avuga ko "... batigeze basaba imbabazi" kubera igitero cyagabwe ku banyagihugu ndetse na bagenzi babo.
Amakuru avuga ko uwakiriye umukino wa tereviziyo yo muri Amerika yerekana Jeopardy!, Alex Trebek w'imyaka 67 ari mu bitaro nyuma yo kurwara umutima muto. Umuvugizi yagize ati: "Alex Trebek, uwakiriye 'Jeopardy!,' Yagize ikibazo cy'umutima gito. Aruhutse neza mu bitaro bya Los Angeles, muri Californiya, kandi azagaruka muri sitidiyo kugira ngo amashusho ateganijwe gukurikira muri Mutarama." kuri iki gitaramo mumatangazo yashyizwe kurubuga rwerekanwa.
Itsinda rito ryaturutse mu Bwongereza Scotland Yard ryageze mu murwa mukuru wa Pakisitani kugira ngo rifashe mu iperereza rya guverinoma ku iyicwa ry’umuyobozi w’abatavuga rumwe n’ubutegetsi Benazir Bhutto. Ijwi rya Nancy-Amelia Collins muri Islamabad rifite byinshi. Abayobozi ba Pakisitani bavuga ko itsinda rya Scotland Yard rizatanga ubumenyi bw’ubucamanza n’ubuhanga mu iperereza rikorwa na guverinoma mu gihe impaka zigenda ziyongera ku rupfu rwa Madamu Bhutto.
Perezida wa Iraki uriho ubu, Jalal Talabani, yavuze ko uwahoze ari perezida Saddam Hussein yemeye ibyaha bitandukanye n'ubwicanyi byakozwe ku butegetsi bwe. Zimwe muri izo manza zirimo gukorwaho iperereza. Bwana Talabani yavuze ko umucamanza yamubwiye aya magambo akekwaho icyaha, yatangaje ko yari abizi kuri televiziyo y'igihugu ya Iraki. Ibisobanuro ni bike, ariko urugero rumwe rwicyaha cyatanzwe ni ubwicanyi bwibasiye imbaga y'Abanyakorde mu mpera za 1980, bikaviramo urupfu rw’Abanyakorde ibihumbi.
JK Rowling, umwanditsi w'uruhererekane rwa "Harry Potter", yatangaje itariki yo gusohora igice cya karindwi kandi cyanyuma - Harry Potter na Hallow Hallows - Ku ya 21 Nyakanga 2007. Mary GrandPre, ushushanya ibitabo bitandatu bya mbere, azagaruka kwerekana ishusho nshya. Igitabo kizasohoka ku isi mu gicuku n’umwanditsi Scholastic. Hateganijwe imbaga nyamwinshi ku isi, kandi igitabo, kuva cyagaragaye bwa mbere kuri Amazon.co.uk, cyariyongereye ku mwanya wa mbere kugurisha mbere yo gutumiza. Igitabo gishya kimaze gutangazwa, Amazon.com yatangaje ko imodoka nyinshi zabaye ku rubuga rwabo. Amazon.com yise igitabo "kimwe mu bitabo bitegerejwe cyane n'ibihe byose"
Ishyamba ryagereranijwe ko rifite ibiti bifite uburebure burenga metero 130. Harimo kandi ibiti bitandukanye bito, ibihuru na fernes. Ibimera bimwe byari bimeze nk'igiti cya asparagus, ariko cyari kingana n'igiti gito. Bikekwa ko ishyamba ryashyinguwe mu mucyo nyuma y’ubutaka bumaze gusunikwa hepfo, munsi y’inyanja, nyuma y’umutingito ukomeye washyinguye ishyamba "ubuziraherezo." Itangazo rigenewe abanyamakuru ryongeyeho riti: "Ishyamba ry’ibimera ryarinzwe nyuma y’umutingito ukomeye mu myaka miriyoni 300 ishize. Umutingito watumye akarere kose kagabanuka munsi y’inyanja aho ishyamba ryashyinguwe mu byondo, rikarindwa iteka."
Indege ya Helios (Boeing 737, indege HCY 522) ifite abagenzi 115 hamwe n’abakozi 6 bari mu bwato yaguye mu musozi saa 09:04 UTC (12:04 pm EEST) hafi ya Grammatiko, ku birometero 40 mu majyaruguru ya Atenayi, ubwo yegeraga ikibuga cy'indege cy'umurwa mukuru. Abari mu bwato bose bararimbutse. Indege yavaga i Larnaca, mu majyepfo y'uburasirazuba bwa Kupuro (Ikigereki: Kypros) ikaba yari iteganijwe kugera i Prague nyuma yo guhagarara muri Atenayi. Ibikorwa byo mu ndege Akimara guhaguruka, abaderevu bavuze ikibazo kijyanye na sisitemu yo guhumeka indege maze basaba kuguma ku butumburuke buke. Nyuma yiminota mike, abapilote bamenyesheje sitasiyo ko ikibazo cyakemutse basaba uruhushya rwo kuzamuka. Aya makuru ariko yahakanye n’umuyobozi wa Helios Airways. Igihe indege yegeraga Atenayi, itumanaho ryose ryarahagaze mu buryo butunguranye, kandi indege ntiyigeze itanga ikimenyetso cy’akababaro. Indege ebyiri za gisirikare zo mu Bugereki F-16 zahawe inshingano zo kureba indege. Abaderevu ba F-16s bavuze ko umuderevu umwe w’indege yasaga nkaho atazi ubwenge undi akaba atari mu kabati.
